 Field Mapping by Event
=======================

This table maps old event types and fields to the New-Scale activity types and fields that correspond to the Common Information Model.

| Old Event | New-Scale Activity Type | Old Fields | New-Scale Fields|
| --------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| dlp-alert | [alert-trigger:success](ActivityTypes/alert-trigger.md) | <br>target_domain<br>user_email<br>attachment<br>attachments<br>recipients<br>subject<br>log_type<br>record_id<br>user_firstname<br>user_fullname<br>sha256_at<br>asset_id<br>user_lastname<br>source<br>logon_id<br>logon_type<br>login_type<br>activity<br>activity_details<br>activity_type<br>parent_sha256hash<br>policy<br>command_line<br>reason<br>rules<br>selected_sha256<br>sender<br>target_sha256<br>full_url | <br>dest_domain<br>email_address<br>email_attachment<br>email_attachments<br>email_recipients<br>email_subject<br>event_category<br>event_id<br>first_name<br>full_name<br>hash_sha256_at<br>host_id<br>last_name<br>legacy_product<br>login_id<br>login_type<br>login_type_text<br>operation<br>operation_details<br>operation_type<br>parent_hash_sha256<br>policy_name<br>process_command_line<br>result_reason<br>rule<br>selected_hash_sha256<br>src_email_address<br>target_hash_sha256<br>url|
